        <script type="text/javascript">
            //JS frame breaker
            if (self === top) {
                document.documentElement.style.display = 'block' ;
            } else {
                top.location = self.location;
            }
            function setUpForDefaultTenant() {
        var $tenantName = $('#tenantName');
        $tenantName.prop("disabled", true);
        $tenantName.attr("value", 'Default');

        $('#createUsernamePassword').fadeSlideUp(500);
        $('#authenticatedTenantFeatures').hide();
        $('#pe-create-tags').hide();
        $('#defaultTenantFeatures').fadeIn(300);
        $('#networkSelectionDiv').hide();
    };
    function setUpForAuthenticatedTenant() {
        $('#tenantName').prop("disabled", false);
        var tenName = document.getElementById("tenantName").value;
        if (tenName == 'Default') {
            $('#tenantName').attr("value", "");
        }

        $('#createUsernamePassword').fadeSlideDown(500);
        $('#defaultTenantFeatures').hide();
        $('#pe-create-tags').fadeIn(300);
        $('#authenticatedTenantFeatures').fadeIn(300);
        $('#networkSelectionDiv').fadeIn(300);
        HCP_ADMIN.Tags.resetTags($("div.tagsPanel", $('#pe-create-tags')));
    };
    function panelShown(key) {
        if (key == 'create') {
            var checked = $('#makeDefaultTenant').prop('checked');
            if (checked) { setUpForDefaultTenant(); }
            else { setUpForAuthenticatedTenant(); }
            
            $('#tenantName').trigger("focus");
        } else if (key == 'create-contact') {
             $('#contactPanelOpenField').val(true);
        } else if (key == 'create-tags') {
             $('#tagsPanelOpenField').val(true);
        }
    }
    function panelHidden(key) {
        if (key == 'create-contact') {
            $('#contactPanelOpenField').val(false);
        } else if (key == 'create-tags') {
            $('#tagsPanelOpenField').val(false);
        }
    }
            $(document).ready(function() {
                initializeLogger(false);
                consoleLog.groupCollapsed("Master Cluster Init");
                consoleLog.time("all javascript masterCluster");
                setTimer(document, 7210, true);
                HCP_ADMIN.startActivityChecker(document, 7210, "/cluster/activityDetected.action");
                $(document).ajaxComplete(function(event,request, settings){
                    var resetTimer = request.getResponseHeader('resetTimer');
                    if (resetTimer != 'false') {
                        setTimer(document, 7210, true);
                        HCP_ADMIN.checkLoggedIn(event, request, settings);
                    }
                });
                // If we receive the startup page as the result of an ajax call, we want
                // to redirect the document to it, not stick it in the middle of the page.
                // Note that we can't use ajaxComplete here since it doesn't get called after
                // we do a load().
                $(document).ajaxSuccess(function(event, request, settings) {
                    var pageName = request.getResponseHeader('Page-Name');
                    if (pageName == 'StartupPage') {
                        // Set completion function to null so jQuery won't try to load content
                        settings.complete = null;
                        document.location.href = "/cluster/systemStartup.action";
                    } else if (pageName == 'ChangePasswordPage') {
                        // Set completion function to null so jQuery won't try to load content
                        settings.complete = null;
                        document.location.href = "/cluster/changePassword_input.action";
                        settings.uri = "/cluster/changePassword_input.action";
                    }
                });
                // If we receive an authorization error as the result of an ajax call, just
                // reload the entire page. That will let the login page be displayed properly.
                $(document).ajaxError(function(event, request, settings) {
                    if (request.status == 401 || request.status == 403) {
                        window.location.reload();
                    }
                });
                //the following is a fix for z-index order for doc and main menus
                var zIndexNumber = 1000;
                $('#docNavWrap, #mainNavWrap').each(function() {
                    $(this).css('zIndex', zIndexNumber);
                    zIndexNumber -= 10;
                });
                initializeSuperfishMenu();
                initializeFixedHeaderTables();
                initializeCheckboxesAndButtons();
                initializeTabIndexes();
                initializeTooltips();
                preloadImages();

                var maxSpanWidth = 150;
                $("#userNameString").createEllipsesIfTooWide(maxSpanWidth, false);
                
                consoleLog.timeEnd("all javascript masterCluster");
                consoleLog.time("all javascript tenants page");
    initializeExpandablePanel(panelShown, panelHidden);
    setUpDynamicTextFillInFromInputField('#tenantName', '#authenticatedTenantNameForLabel', '#createCancel');
    
    
    
    

    $('#createCancelDiv').on("click", function() { setUpForAuthenticatedTenant(); });
    $('#makeDefaultTenant').on('change', function() {
        var checked = $(this).prop('checked');

        if (checked) { setUpForDefaultTenant(); }
        else { setUpForAuthenticatedTenant(); }
    });
    $('input.authScheme').on('change', function() {
        if ($(this).val() == 'LOCAL') {
            $('#externalUser').fadeOut('fast', function() {
                $('#localUser').fadeIn('fast');
            });
        } else {
            $('#localUser').fadeOut('fast', function() {
                $('#externalUser').fadeIn('fast');
            });
        }
    });

    $('.selectServicePlans').on("click", function() {
        var inputId = $(this).prev('input').attr('id');
        if ( !$('#' + inputId).prop('disabled') ) {
            showFixedOverlay(this, $(this).attr('rdiv'), '870px', 'Select Service Plan', '_top');
        }
        return false;
    });

    $('#manageTagsTenantsId').on("click", function() {
        showOverlay(this, $(this).attr('rdiv'), '870px', 'Tags', '_top');

        return false;
    });
                consoleLog.groupEnd("Master Cluster Init");
            });
        </script>

<script type="text/javascript">

  $(function() {
    initializeCheckboxesAndButtons("#createTenant");
    initializeForm('createTenant');

    var $authLocal = $('#localAuthentication');
    var $authAD = $('#activeDirectory');
    var $authLOCAL = $('#authSchemeValue_LOCAL');
    var $authEXTERNAL = $('#authSchemeValue_EXTERNAL');

    syncSecurityControls();

    $('#createSubmit').on("click", function () {
        var formId = "#createTenant";
        var dplValue = $('#dplSelectBox').val();
        if ((dplValue != undefined && (dplValue == '1' || (dplValue.startsWith('Dynamic') && '2' == '1')))
                && true && true && $('#makeDefaultTenant').prop('checked')) {
            $('#confirmField').val(false);
            var title = "Namespace Protection Level";
            var critical = "With a DPL of one, it is highly recommended that all directories in the " +
                           "namespace be replicated.";
            var buttonText = "Create Tenant";
            overlayConfirmSubmit(title, null, formId, buttonText, null, critical, null, false, true);
        } else {
            $('#confirmField').val(true);
            $(formId).trigger('submit');
        }
    });


    var $ecSelectedNamespacesId = $('#ecSelectedNamespacesId');
    var $replicationEnabled = $('#replicationEnabled');

    // Hide EC selection on initial page load if replication not enabled
    if (!$replicationEnabled.prop('checked')) {
        $ecSelectedNamespacesId.hide();
    }

    // Adjust the EC setting when replication setting is changed
    $replicationEnabled.on('change', function() {
        $this = $(this);
        if ($this.prop('checked')) {
            $ecSelectedNamespacesId.show();
        } else {
            $ecSelectedNamespacesId.hide();
        }
    });

    $('#noNamespaceQuota').on('change', function() {
        $this = $(this);
        $namespaceQuota = $('#namespaceQuota');
        if ($this.prop('checked')) {
            $namespaceQuota.val('');
            $namespaceQuota.prop('disabled', true);
        } else {
            $namespaceQuota.prop('disabled', false);
            $namespaceQuota.val('');
        }
    });


    $('#servicePlansEnabled').on('change', function() {
        $this = $(this);
        var textBox = jQuery('#servicePlansSelectId');
        if ($this.prop('checked')) {
            textBox.hide();
            textBox.val('Default');

            $("div#authenticatedTenantFeatures .selectServicePlans").hide();
            $("div#authenticatedTenantFeatures .overlaySelection").hide();
        } else {
            textBox.show();

            $("div#authenticatedTenantFeatures .selectServicePlans").show();
            $("div#authenticatedTenantFeatures .overlaySelection").show();
        }
    });
    
    $('.jQueryAuthMethod').on('change', function() {
        syncSecurityControls($(this));
    });
    
    function syncSecurityControls(control) {
        var adEnabledAndConfigured = $('#adEnabledAndConfigured').val();
        var local = $authLocal.is(':checked')
        var ad = $authAD.is(':checked')
        if(control != undefined) {
            if(control.attr('id') == 'localAuthentication') {
                $authAD.prop('checked', true);
                ad = true;
            }  
            else {
                $authLocal.prop('checked', true);
                local = true;
            }
        }
        if(local && !ad) {
            $authEXTERNAL.prop('disabled', true);

            $authLOCAL.prop('disabled', false);
            $authLOCAL.prop('checked', true);
            $authLOCAL.trigger("change");
        }
        else if(ad && !local) {
            $authLOCAL.prop('disabled', true);

            if ( adEnabledAndConfigured == "true") {
                $authEXTERNAL.prop('disabled', false);
                $authEXTERNAL.prop('checked', true);
                $authEXTERNAL.trigger("change");
            } 
        }
        else {
            $authLOCAL.prop('disabled', false);

             if ( adEnabledAndConfigured == "true") {
                $authEXTERNAL.prop('disabled', false);
             }
        }
        fixCheckboxes('.jQueryAuthMethod', $('.securityAccountCreate_top'));
        fixCheckboxes('.authScheme', $('.securityAccountCreate_top'));
    }

    /* the code below ensures that when create tenant fails, and if "No quota" checkbox is checked,
       the namespace quota textfield is grayed out and blank.
     */
    var nsChecked = $('#noNamespaceQuota').is(':checked');
    if (nsChecked == true) {
        $('#namespaceQuota').prop('disabled', true);
    } 
  });
</script>

    $(".allownumericwithComma").on("keypress keyup blur", function (event) {
        $(this).val($(this).val().replace(/[^0-9\,]/g, ''));
        if ((event.which != 44) && (event.which < 48 || event.which > 57)) {
            event.preventDefault();
        }
    });

    $(".allownumericwithComma").on("keypress keyup blur", function (event) {
        $(this).val($(this).val().replace(/[^0-9\,]/g, ''));
        if ((event.which != 44) && (event.which < 48 || event.which > 57)) {
            event.preventDefault();

<script type="text/javascript">
    $(function() {
        // reload the services every 10 seconds
        $('#policyStatus').stopTime("updatePolicies");
        $('#policyStatus').oneTime(10000, "updatePolicies", function() {
            $('#policyStatus').load('/cluster/currentPolicyStatus.action?resetIdleTimeout=false');
        });


        $('.serviceContol').on("click", function () {
            $('#policyStatus').load($(this).attr('rdiv'), function(response, status) {
                if (status == "error") {
                    HCP_ADMIN.showErrorMessageFromResponseInStatus(response, null, "updateStatus");
                }
            });
        });
    });
</script>
